Lingaguessr Audio Corpus — Handoff & Methodology

Generated 2026-06-04 13:09 · 40 languages · 1506 YouTube clips

What this is

A purpose-built corpus of natural-speech audio clips (~19s each) sourced directly from YouTube for the major world languages in the game. It replaces the thin single-word / short-sentence open-source recordings (Lingua Libre, FLEURS) for those languages with real connected speech — news bulletins, interviews, podcasts, audiobooks — so players hear how each language actually sounds in the wild. English is excluded by design.

Methodology

  1. Discovery. Candidates were found with yt-dlp's native YouTube search (ytsearch) using the ios player client, which plays past YouTube's anonymous bot-wall. Each language used curated native-language queries (e.g. Hindi हिंदी समाचार बुलेटिन, Japanese ニュース 日本 解説) to bias results toward monolingual, on-topic speech. (Browser-cookie and Invidious routes were tried and rejected: Chrome/Brave cookies are app-bound-encrypted and rotate; public Invidious instances returned 401/403.)
  2. Download. Only a --download-sections 15-20s window was pulled — audio only — at an offset 25-50% into each video to skip intros/music, extracted to MP3 via ffmpeg.
  3. Transcription & language verification. Every candidate clip was transcribed with MLX Whisper (whisper-large-v3-turbo) in auto-detect mode. A clip is accepted only if Whisper's detected language matches the target and the transcript clears a length floor — filtering out music, English voice-overs, wrong-language hits, and silence.
  4. Provenance. Each accepted clip stores its transcript and exact source URL (with a &t=<start>s timestamp) in manifest.json and in the table below.

Rebuild / extend

Pipeline: audio_corpus_builder/build_corpus.py (discover→download→Whisper-verify→ write, resumable) then audio_corpus_builder/finalize.py (merge into manifest + this doc). Re-run one language: python3 build_corpus.py hin. Tunables (TARGET clips, CLIP_LEN, per-language QUERIES) are at the top of the script. A backup of the prior manifest is at public/manifest.json.bak.*.
